<state_snapshot>
    <overall_goal>
        Create a Node.js utility using TypeScript and pnpm to scrape cabin information from the finn.no website.
    </overall_goal>

    <key_knowledge>
        - The target website, finn.no, is heavily reliant on client-side JavaScript and makes extensive use of custom elements with **Shadow DOM**.
        - Initial scraping attempts with `axios` and `cheerio` failed because they do not process the fully rendered page or access the Shadow DOM.
        - The project has been refactored to use `puppeteer` to control a headless Chrome browser, which can render the JavaScript.
        - Even with `puppeteer`, simply parsing the main page content with `cheerio` is ineffective for most data points because they are encapsulated within the Shadow DOM.
        - The next attempt must focus on either querying inside the Shadow DOM using Puppeteer's `page.evaluate()` or finding a structured data source (like a `&lt;script type="application/ld+json"&gt;` tag) embedded in the page.
        - A 1-second delay between requests must be maintained to avoid rate limiting.
    </key_knowledge>

    <file_system_state>
        - CWD: `/Users/remi/source/finn-scrapper`
        - MODIFIED: `package.json` - Added dependencies `axios`, `cheerio`, `puppeteer`, and configured `"type": "module"`.
        - MODIFIED: `tsconfig.json` - Configured for an ES module project.
        - MODIFIED: `src/main.ts` - Contains the current `puppeteer`-based scraping logic. It successfully launches the browser, navigates, and extracts property URLs, but fails to extract most of the specific details from the property pages.
        - READ: Temporary HTML files (e.g., `puppeteer_output_*.html`) saved in `/Users/remi/.gemini/tmp/6e35c2bf80016cd7913d6eb8bb70141429367cc63a881bfdc9938286ac16aa0f/`. Analysis of these files led to the discovery of the Shadow DOM issue.
    </file_system_state>

    <recent_actions>
        - Ran the `src/main.ts` script using `ts-node`.
        - The script successfully used `puppeteer` to navigate to a property page and save its full HTML content to a file.
        - The data extraction for most fields (`price`, `address`, `description`, etc.) returned `null`.
        - Read the saved HTML file (`puppeteer_output_1763548450185.html`).
        - Concluded from the HTML structure that the scraping failure is due to the target data being inside the Shadow DOM of custom web components, which `cheerio` cannot access from the main document.
    </recent_actions>

    <current_plan>
        1. [DONE] Set up the Node.js TypeScript project with pnpm.

        3. [DONE] Implement basic search page scraping and pagination to get property links.
        4. [DONE] Switch from `axios`/`cheerio` to `puppeteer` to handle client-side rendering.
        5. [DONE] Install and configure `puppeteer`.
        6. [IN PROGRESS] Refactor the property detail scraping logic (`fetchPropertyDetails` function in `src/main.ts`) to correctly extract data from the finn.no page. The current implementation is failing.

Ditching `page.content()` for `page.evaluate()` will let me access the fully rendered DOM, including Shadow DOM, and interact with it directly. ‚ú® ## MODEL

Okay, I'm refactoring `src/main.ts`. I'll switch `fetchPropertyDetails` to `page.evaluate()` to leverage the browser's DOM and will also remove the temp file saving logic.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import * as cheerio from 'cheerio';\nimport puppeteer from 'puppeteer';\nimport { Browser, Page } from 'puppeteer';\n\nconst BASE_URL = \"https://www.finn.no/realestate/leisuresale/search.html?filters=\";\n\ninterface PropertyDetails {\n    url: string;\n    finnCode: string | null;\n    price: string | null;\n    address: string | null;\n    description: string | null;\n    facilities: string[] | null;\n    winterSports: boolean;\n    summerActivities: boolean;\n    altitude: string | null;\n    images: string[];\n    exploreLink: string | null;\n    exploreDetails: any; // To store additional data from explore link\n}\n\nlet browser: Browser;\n\nasync function initializeBrowser() {\n    browser = await puppeteer.launch({ headless: true });\n}\n\nasync function closeBrowser() {\n    await browser.close();\n}\n\nasync function fetchPageContent(url: string, waitForSelector?: string): Promise<string | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });\n        if (waitForSelector) {\n            await page.waitForSelector(waitForSelector, { timeout: 10000 }); // Wait up to 10 seconds\n        }\n        const content = await page.content();\n        return content;\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching page content from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchSearchResults(url: string): Promise<{ propertyLinks: string[], nextPageLink: string | null }> {\n    const propertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let nextPageLink: string | null = null;\n\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]');\n    if (!content) {\n        return { propertyLinks: [], nextPageLink: null };\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n\n    $('main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]').each((i, element) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link) {\n            const fullLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            propertyLinks.push(fullLink);\n        }\n    });\n    console.log(`Found ${propertyLinks.length} property links on ${url}`);\n\n    $('nav[aria-label=\"Pagination\"] a[title=\"Neste side\"]').each((i, element) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link) {\n            nextPageLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            return false;\n        }\n    });\n\n    return { propertyLinks, nextPageLink };\n}\n\nasync function fetchPropertyDetails(url: string): Promise<PropertyDetails | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'networkidle2' }); // Wait for network to be idle\n        \n        const details: Omit<PropertyDetails, 'url' | 'finnCode' | 'exploreLink'> & { finnCode: string | null, url: string, exploreLink: string | null } = await page.evaluate(() => {\n            const getElementText = (selector: string) => document.querySelector(selector)?.textContent?.trim() || null;\n            const getElementAttribute = (selector: string, attribute: string) => document.querySelector(selector)?.getAttribute(attribute) || null;\n\n            const price = getElementText('div[data-testid=\"price-suggestion\"] dd');\n            const address = getElementText('main p.mt-4.text-18');\n            const description = getElementText('div.udt-description-text');\n            \n            const facilities: string[] = [];\n            document.querySelectorAll('section[aria-labelledby=\"facilities-heading\"] dt').forEach(el => {\n                if (el.textContent) {\n                    facilities.push(el.textContent.trim());\n                }\n            });\n\n            let winterSports = false;\n            let summerActivities = false;\n\n            const beliggenhet = getElementText('div[data-testid=\"info-situation\"] dd');\n            if (beliggenhet && beliggenhet.includes(\"fjellet\")) {\n                winterSports = true;\n            }\n            \n            const altitude = getElementText('div[data-testid=\"area-profile-property-item-altitude\"] dd');\n            if (altitude) {\n                const altitudeValue = parseInt(altitude.replace(/[^0-9]/g, ''));\n                if (altitudeValue > 500) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (facilities) {\n                if (facilities.some(f => f.includes(\"Bademulighet\") || f.includes(\"Fiskemulighet\") || f.includes(\"strand\"))) {\n                    summerActivities = true;\n                }\n                if (facilities.some(f => f.includes(\"Alpinanlegg\") || f.includes(\"skil√∏ype\"))) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            const images: string[] = [];\n            document.querySelectorAll('section[aria-label=\"Bildegalleri\"] img[data-srcset]').forEach(el => {\n                const srcset = el.getAttribute('data-srcset');\n                if (srcset) {\n                    const urls = srcset.split(',').map(s => s.trim().split(' ')[0]);\n                    const largestUrl = urls[urls.length - 1];\n                    if (largestUrl) {\n                        images.push(largestUrl);\n                    }\n                }\n            });\n\n            const exploreLink = getElementAttribute('section[aria-label=\"Om stedet\"] a:contains(\"Utforsk\")', 'href');\n\n            return {\n                price,\n                address,\n                description,\n                facilities,\n                winterSports,\n                summerActivities,\n                altitude,\n                images,\n                exploreLink,\n                finnCode: null, // finnCode is extracted from url later\n                url: '', // url is added later\n                exploreDetails: null, // exploreDetails is added later\n            };\n        });\n\n        const finnCodeMatch = url.match(/finnkode=(\\d+)/);\n        details.finnCode = finnCodeMatch ? finnCodeMatch[1] : null;\n        details.url = url;\n\n        if (details.exploreLink) {\n            details.exploreDetails = await fetchExploreDetails(details.exploreLink);\n            if (details.exploreDetails.altitudeFromExplore && !details.altitude) {\n                details.altitude = details.exploreDetails.altitudeFromExplore;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return details;\n\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching property details from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchExploreDetails(url: string): Promise<any> {\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'body'); // General selector\n    if (!content) {\n        console.error(`Failed to get explore details content for ${url}.`);\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n    const details: any = {};\n\n    // Example: Extract altitude if present on this page\n    const altitudeElement = $('div[data-testid=\"area-profile-property-item-altitude\"] dd');\n    if (altitudeElement.length > 0) {\n        details.altitudeFromExplore = altitudeElement.text().trim();\n    }\n\n    return details;\n}\n\nasync function scrapeAllPages(startUrl: string) {\n    await initializeBrowser();\n    let currentUrl: string | null = startUrl;\n    let allPropertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let pageCount = 0;\n\n    try {\n        while (currentUrl && pageCount < 1) { // Limiting to 1 page for faster debugging\n            pageCount++;\n            console.log(`Scraping page ${pageCount}: ${currentUrl}`);\n            const { propertyLinks, nextPageLink } = await fetchSearchResults(currentUrl);\n            allPropertyLinks = allPropertyLinks.concat(propertyLinks);\n            currentUrl = nextPageLink;\n            if (currentUrl) {\n                console.log(`Waiting for 1 second before fetching next page...`);\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 second delay\n            }\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allPropertyLinks.length} property links.`);\n        console.log(\"All Extracted Property Links:\", allPropertyLinks);\n\n        // Fetch details for the first property (for debugging)\n        if (allPropertyLinks.length > 0) {\n            const link = allPropertyLinks[0];\n            if (link) {\n                const details = await fetchPropertyDetails(link);\n                console.log(`Details for ${link}:`, details);\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n",
    "file_path": "src/main.ts"
  }
}

‚ú® ## MODEL

I have a `SyntaxError` because `:contains()` is a jQuery extension, not a valid `querySelector`. I need to iterate `a` tags within `section[aria-label="Om stedet"]`, check their `textContent`, and find the "Utforsk" link. I will update `src/main.ts` to implement this.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/main.ts",
    "content": "import * as cheerio from 'cheerio';\nimport puppeteer from 'puppeteer';\nimport { Browser, Page } from 'puppeteer';\n\nconst BASE_URL = \"https://www.finn.no/realestate/leisuresale/search.html?filters=\";\n\ninterface PropertyDetails {\n    url: string;\n    finnCode: string | null;\n    price: string | null;\n    address: string | null;\n    description: string | null;\n    facilities: string[] | null;\n    winterSports: boolean;\n    summerActivities: boolean;\n    altitude: string | null;\n    images: string[];\n    exploreLink: string | null;\n    exploreDetails: any; // To store additional data from explore link\n}\n\nlet browser: Browser;\n\nasync function initializeBrowser() {\n    browser = await puppeteer.launch({ headless: true });\n}\n\nasync function closeBrowser() {\n    await browser.close();\n}\n\nasync function fetchPageContent(url: string, waitForSelector?: string): Promise<string | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });\n        if (waitForSelector) {\n            await page.waitForSelector(waitForSelector, { timeout: 10000 }); // Wait up to 10 seconds\n        }\n        const content = await page.content();\n        return content;\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching page content from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchSearchResults(url: string): Promise<{ propertyLinks: string[], nextPageLink: string | null }> {\n    const propertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let nextPageLink: string | null = null;\n\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]');\n    if (!content) {\n        return { propertyLinks: [], nextPageLink: null };\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n\n    $('main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]').each((i, element) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link) {\n            const fullLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            propertyLinks.push(fullLink);\n        }\n    });\n    console.log(`Found ${propertyLinks.length} property links on ${url}`);\n\n    $('nav[aria-label=\"Pagination\"] a[title=\"Neste side\"]').each((i, element) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link) {\n            nextPageLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            return false;\n        }\n    });\n\n    return { propertyLinks, nextPageLink };\n}\n\nasync function fetchPropertyDetails(url: string): Promise<PropertyDetails | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'networkidle2' }); // Wait for network to be idle\n        \n        const details: Omit<PropertyDetails, 'url' | 'finnCode' | 'exploreLink'> & { finnCode: string | null, url: string, exploreLink: string | null } = await page.evaluate(() => {\n            const getElementText = (selector: string) => document.querySelector(selector)?.textContent?.trim() || null;\n\n            const price = getElementText('div[data-testid=\"price-suggestion\"] dd');\n            const address = getElementText('main p.mt-4.text-18');\n            const description = getElementText('div.udt-description-text');\n            \n            const facilities: string[] = [];\n            document.querySelectorAll('section[aria-labelledby=\"facilities-heading\"] dt').forEach(el => {\n                if (el.textContent) {\n                    facilities.push(el.textContent.trim());\n                }\n            });\n\n            let winterSports = false;\n            let summerActivities = false;\n\n            const beliggenhet = getElementText('div[data-testid=\"info-situation\"] dd');\n            if (beliggenhet && beliggenhet.includes(\"fjellet\")) {\n                winterSports = true;\n            }\n            \n            const altitude = getElementText('div[data-testid=\"area-profile-property-item-altitude\"] dd');\n            if (altitude) {\n                const altitudeValue = parseInt(altitude.replace(/[^0-9]/g, ''));\n                if (altitudeValue > 500) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (facilities) {\n                if (facilities.some(f => f.includes(\"Bademulighet\") || f.includes(\"Fiskemulighet\") || f.includes(\"strand\"))) {\n                    summerActivities = true;\n                }\n                if (facilities.some(f => f.includes(\"Alpinanlegg\") || f.includes(\"skil√∏ype\"))) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n            }\n            \n            const images: string[] = [];\n            document.querySelectorAll('section[aria-label=\"Bildegalleri\"] img[data-srcset]').forEach(el => {\n                const srcset = el.getAttribute('data-srcset');\n                if (srcset) {\n                    const urls = srcset.split(',').map(s => s.trim().split(' ')[0]);\n                    const largestUrl = urls[urls.length - 1];\n                    if (largestUrl) {\n                        images.push(largestUrl);\n                    }\n                }\n            });\n            \n            let exploreLink: string | null = null;\n            const exploreLinks = document.querySelectorAll('section[aria-label=\"Om stedet\"] a');\n            for(const link of Array.from(exploreLinks)){\n                if(link.textContent?.trim() === \"Utforsk\"){\n                    exploreLink = (link as HTMLAnchorElement).href;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n            \n\n            return {\n                price,\n                address,\n                description,\n                facilities,\n                winterSports,\n                summerActivities,\n                altitude,\n                images,\n                exploreLink,\n                finnCode: null, // finnCode is extracted from url later\n                url: '', // url is added later\n                exploreDetails: null, // exploreDetails is added later\n            };\n        });\n\n        const finnCodeMatch = url.match(/finnkode=(\\d+)/);\n        details.finnCode = finnCodeMatch ? finnCodeMatch[1] : null;\n        details.url = url;\n\n        if (details.exploreLink) {\n            details.exploreDetails = await fetchExploreDetails(details.exploreLink);\n            if (details.exploreDetails.altitudeFromExplore && !details.altitude) {\n                details.altitude = details.exploreDetails.altitudeFromExplore;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return details;\n\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching property details from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchExploreDetails(url: string): Promise<any> {\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'body'); // General selector\n    if (!content) {\n        console.error(`Failed to get explore details content for ${url}.`);\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n    const details: any = {};\n\n    // Example: Extract altitude if present on this page\n    const altitudeElement = $('div[data-testid=\"area-profile-property-item-altitude\"] dd');\n    if (altitudeElement.length > 0) {\n        details.altitudeFromExplore = altitudeElement.text().trim();\n    }\n\n    return details;\n}\n\nasync function scrapeAllPages(startUrl: string) {\n    await initializeBrowser();\n    let currentUrl: string | null = startUrl;\n    let allPropertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let pageCount = 0;\n\n    try {\n        while (currentUrl && pageCount < 1) { // Limiting to 1 page for faster debugging\n            pageCount++;\n            console.log(`Scraping page ${pageCount}: ${currentUrl}`);\n            const { propertyLinks, nextPageLink } = await fetchSearchResults(currentUrl);\n            allPropertyLinks = allPropertyLinks.concat(propertyLinks);\n            currentUrl = nextPageLink;\n            if (currentUrl) {\n                console.log(`Waiting for 1 second before fetching next page...`);\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 second delay\n            }\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allPropertyLinks.length} property links.`);\n        console.log(\"All Extracted Property Links:\", allPropertyLinks);\n\n        // Fetch details for the first property (for debugging)\n        if (allPropertyLinks.length > 0) {\n            const link = allPropertyLinks[0];\n            if (link) {\n                const details = await fetchPropertyDetails(link);\n                console.log(`Details for ${link}:`, details);\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n"
  }
}

‚ú® ## MODEL

`page.evaluate()` seems to work, but my selectors are failing to extract most data. I'll debug this by adding `console.log` statements inside the `page.evaluate()` block to inspect values directly. I'll also add a `console` event listener to my Puppeteer page to see the browser logs in my terminal, and I'll change the `waitForSelector` to `main`.**Tool Command**:

null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        page.on('console', msg => console.log('PAGE LOG:', msg.text()));\n        await page.goto(url, { }> {\n    const propertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let nextPageLink: string | null = null;\n\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]');\n    if (!content)        description,\n                facilities,\n                winterSports,\n                summerActivities,\n                altitude,\n                images,\n                exploreLink,\n                finnCode: null,\n                url: '',\n                exploreDetails: null,\n            };\n        });\n\n        const finnCodeMatch = url.match(/finnkode=(\\d+)/);\n        details.finnCode = finnCodeMatch ? finnCodeMatch[1] : null;\n        details.url = url;\n\n        if (details.exploreLink) {\n            details.exploreDetails = await fetchExploreDetails(details.exploreLink);\n            if (details.exploreDetails.altitudeFromExplore && !details.altitude) {\n                details.altitude = details.exploreDetails.altitudeFromExplore;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return details;\n\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching property details from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchExploreDetails(url: string): Promise<any> {\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'body'); // General selector\n    if (!content) {\n        console.error(`Failed to get explore details content for ${url}.`);\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n    const details: any = {};\n\n    const altitudeElement = $('div[data-testid=\"area-profile-property-item-altitude\"] dd');\n    if (altitudeElement.length > 0) {\n        details.altitudeFromExplore = altitudeElement.text().trim();\n    }\n\n    return details;\n}\n\nasync function scrapeAllPages(startUrl: string) {\n    await initializeBrowser();\n    let currentUrl: string | null = startUrl;\n    let allPropertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let pageCount = 0;\n\n    try {\n        while (currentUrl && pageCount < 1) { // Limiting to 1 page for faster debugging\n            pageCount++;\n            console.log(`Scraping page ${pageCount}: ${currentUrl}`);\n            const { propertyLinks, nextPageLink } = await fetchSearchResults(currentUrl);\n            allPropertyLinks = allPropertyLinks.concat(propertyLinks);\n            currentUrl = nextPageLink;\n            if (currentUrl) {\n                console.log(`Waiting for 1 second before fetching next page...`);\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 second delay\n            }\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allPropertyLinks.length} property links.`);\n        console.log(\"All Extracted Property Links:\", allPropertyLinks);\n\n        // Fetch details for the first property (for debugging)\n        if (allPropertyLinks.length > 0) {\n            const link = allPropertyLinks[0];\n            if (link) {\n                const details = await fetchPropertyDetails(link);\n                console.log(`Details for ${link}:`, details);\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n"
  }
}
```

fetchSearchResults(url: string): Promise<{ propertyLinks: string[], nextPageLink: string | null }> {\n    const propertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let nextPageLink: string | null = null;\n\n    const fetchPropertyDetails(url: string): Promise<PropertyDetails | null> {\n    const {content, fileName} = await fetchPageContent(url, 'body'); // Use body as a general selector\n    if (!content) {\n        console.error(`Failed to get content for ${url}. See ${fileName} if available.`);\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n    console.log(\"Successfully fetched and parsed property details page.\");\n\n    const finnCodeMatch = url.match(/finnkode=(\\d+)/);\n    const finnCode = finnCodeMatch ? finnCodeMatch[1] : null;\n\n    let price: string | null = null;\n    let address: string | null = null;\n    let description: string | null = null;\n    let facilities: string[] = [];\n    let winterSports = false;\n    let summerActivities = false;\n    let altitude: string | null = null;\n    let images: string[] = [];\n    let exploreLink: string | null = null;\n\n    const nextData = $('script#__NEXT_DATA__').html();\n    if (nextData) {\n        try {\n            const data = JSON.parse(nextData);\n            const ad = data.props.pageProps.ad;\n            \n            price = ad.price?.value.toString() || null;\n            address = ad.location.address;\n            description = ad.description;\n            \n            facilities = ad.facilities.map((f: any) => f.label);\n\n            if(ad.location.altitude) {\n                altitude = ad.location.altitude.toString();\n                if(ad.location.altitude > 500) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (facilities.some(f => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"bademulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"fiskemulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"strand\"))) {\n                summerActivities = true;\n            }\n            if (facilities.some(f => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"alpinanlegg\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"skil√∏ype\"))) {\n                winterSports = true;\n            }\n            \n            images = ad.media.map((m: any) => m.url);\n            \n            exploreLink = ad.areaProfileUrl;\n\n        } catch (error) {\n            console.error(\"Error parsing __NEXT_DATA__\", error);\n        }\n    }\n\n\n    const details: PropertyDetails = {\n        url: url,\n        finnCode: finnCode,\n        price: price,\n        address: address,\n        description: description,\n        facilities: facilities.length > 0 ?   }

‚ú® ## MODEL

`waitForSelector` is failing on the property page. I'll modify `src/main.ts` to disable `__NEXT_DATA__` parsing and use `page.evaluate` to get the body's `outerHTML`, which I'll then log to the console for inspection to find the correct selectors.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import * as cheerio from 'cheerio';\nimport puppeteer from 'puppeteer';\nimport { Browser, Page } from 'puppeteer';\nimport * as fs from 'fs/promises';\n\nconst BASE_URL = \"https://www.finn.no/realestate/leisuresale/search.html?filters=\";\n\ninterface PropertyDetails {\n    url: string;\n    finnCode: string | null;\n    price: string | null;\n    address: string | null;\n    description: string | null;\n    facilities: string[] | null;\n    winterSports: boolean;\n    summerActivities: boolean;\n    altitude: string | null;\n    images: string[];\n    exploreLink: string | null;\n    exploreDetails: any; // To store additional data from explore link\n}\n\nlet browser: Browser;\n\nasync function initializeBrowser() {\n    browser = await puppeteer.launch({ headless: true });\n}\n\nasync function closeBrowser() {\n    await browser.close();\n}\n\nasync function fetchPageContent(url: string, waitForSelector?: string): Promise<string | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });\n        if (waitForSelector) {\n            await page.waitForSelector(waitForSelector, { timeout: 10000 }); // Wait up to 10 seconds\n        }\n        const content = await page.content();\n        return content;\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching page content from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchSearchResults(url: string): Promise<{ propertyLinks: string[], nextPageLink: string | null }> {\n    const propertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let nextPageLink: string | null = null;\n\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]');\n    if (!content) {\n        return { propertyLinks: [], nextPageLink: null };\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n\n    $('main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]').each((i, element) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link) {\n            const fullLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            propertyLinks.push(fullLink);\n        }\n    });\n    console.log(`Found ${propertyLinks.length} property links on ${url}`);\n\n    $('nav[aria-label=\"Pagination\"] a[title=\"Neste side\"]').each((i, element) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link) {\n            nextPageLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            return false;\n        }\n    });\n\n    return { propertyLinks, nextPageLink };\n}\n\nasync function fetchPropertyDetails(url: string): Promise<any> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'networkidle2' });\n        const bodyHTML = await page.evaluate(() => document.body.outerHTML);\n        console.log(bodyHTML);\n        return null; // Return null for now, just to inspect the HTML\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching property details from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n\nasync function scrapeAllPages(startUrl: string) {\n    await initializeBrowser();\n    let currentUrl: string | null = startUrl;\n    let allPropertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let pageCount = 0;\n\n    try {\n        while (currentUrl && pageCount < 1) { // Limiting to 1 page for faster debugging\n            pageCount++;\n            console.log(`Scraping page ${pageCount}: ${currentUrl}`);\n            const { propertyLinks, nextPageLink } = await fetchSearchResults(currentUrl);\n            allPropertyLinks = allPropertyLinks.concat(propertyLinks);\n            currentUrl = nextPageLink;\n            if (currentUrl) {\n                console.log(`Waiting for 1 second before fetching next page...`);\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 second delay\n            }\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allPropertyLinks.length} property links.`);\n        console.log(\"All Extracted Property Links:\", allPropertyLinks);\n\n        // Fetch details for the first property (for debugging)\n        if (allPropertyLinks.length > 0) {\n            const link = allPropertyLinks[0];\n            if (link) {\n                await fetchPropertyDetails(link);\n            }\n        }\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n",
    "file_path": "src/main.ts"
  }

‚ú® ## MODEL

I have a `ReferenceError` because I'm in an ES module and used `require`. I'll fix this by replacing `require('cheerio')` with an `import * as cheerio from 'cheerio'` statement at the top of `src/main.ts` and then using `const $ = cheerio.load(content)` where needed.**Tool Command**:

‚ú® ## MODEL

Found `__NEXT_DATA__` at `props.pageProps.ad` in the property details HTML. Updating `src/main.ts` to parse this JSON, then removing temporary code.**Tool Command**:
```json

summerActivities: summerActivities,\n                altitude: altitude,\n                images: images,\n                exploreLink: exploreLink,\n            };\n\n        } catch (error) {\n fetchPropertyDetails(link);\n                if (details) {\n                    allDetails.push(details);\n                }\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 second delay\n            }\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allDetails.length} properties.`);\n        \n        // Save the final JSON data to a file\n        await fs.writeFile('properties.json', JSON.stringify(allDetails, null, 2));\n        console.log('Saved data to properties.json');\n\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n",

data.props.pageProps.ad;\n\n            const finnCodeMatch = url.match(/finnkode=(\\d+)/);\n            const finnCode = finnCodeMatch ? finnCodeMatch[1] : null;\n\n            const price = ad.price?.value.toString() || null;\n            const address = ad.location.address;\n            const description = ad.description;\n            \n            const facilities = ad.facilities.map((f: any) => f.label);\n\n            let winterSports = false;\n            let summerActivities = false;\n            let altitude: string | null = null;\n\n            if (ad.location.altitude) {\n                altitude = ad.location.altitude.toString();\n                if (ad.location.altitude > 500) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n url: url,\n                finnCode: finnCode,\n                price: price,\n                address: address,\n                description: description,\n                facilities: facilities.length > 0 ? facilities : null,\n                winterSports: winterSports,\n                summerActivities: summerActivities,\n                altitude: altitude,\n ```json

const ad = data.props.pageProps.ad;\n\n                const finnCodeMatch = url.match(/finnkode=(\\d+)/);\n                const finnCode = finnCodeMatch ? finnCodeMatch[1] : null;\n\n                const price = ad.price?.value.toString() || null;\n                const address = ad.location.address;\n                const description = ad.description;\n                \n                const facilities = ad.facilities.map((f: any) => f.label);\n\n                let winterSports = false;\n                let summerActivities = false;\n                let altitude: string | null = null;\n\n                if (ad.location.altitude) {\n                    altitude = ad.location.altitude.toString();\n                    if (ad.location.altitude > 500) {\n                        winterSports = true;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (facilities.some((f: string) => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"bademulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"fiskemulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"strand\"))) {\n                    summerActivities = true;\n                }\n                if (facilities.some((f: string) => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"alpinanlegg\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"skil√∏ype\"))) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n\n                const images = ad.media.map((m: any) => m.url);\n                const exploreLink = ad.areaProfileUrl;\n\n                return {\n                    url: url,\n                    finnCode: finnCode,\n                    price: price,\n                    address: address,\n                    description: description,\n                    facilities: facilities.length > 0 ? facilities : null,\n                    winterSports: winterSports,\n                    summerActivities: summerActivities,\n                    altitude: altitude,\n                    images: images,\n                    exploreLink: exploreLink,\n                };\n\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\"Error parsing __NEXT_DATA__\", error);\n                return null;\n            }\n        }\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching property details from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\nasync function scrapeAllPages(startUrl: string) {\n    await initializeBrowser();\n    let currentUrl: string | null = startUrl;\n    const allDetails: PropertyDetails[] = [];\n\n    try {\n        while (currentUrl) {\n            console.log(`Scraping page: ${currentUrl}`);\n            const { propertyLinks, nextPageLink } = await fetchSearchResults(currentUrl);\n\n            for (const link of propertyLinks) {\n                const details = await fetchPropertyDetails(link);\n                if (details) {\n                    allDetails.push(details);\n                }\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 second delay\n            }\n\n            currentUrl = nextPageLink;\n            if (currentUrl) {\n                console.log(`Waiting for 1 second before fetching next page...`);\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 second delay\n            }\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allDetails.length} properties.`);\n        \n        await fs.writeFile('properties.json', JSON.stringify(allDetails, null, 2));\n        console.log('Saved data to properties.json');\n\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n",
    "file_path": "src/main.ts"
  }
}
```

null;\n    description: string | null;\n    facilities: string[] | null;\n    winterSports: boolean;\n    summerActivities: boolean;\n    altitude: string | null;\n    images: string[];\n {
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {

\"https://www.finn.no/realestate/leisuresale/search.html?filters=\";\n\ninterface PropertyDetails {\n    url: string;\n    finnCode: string | null;\n    price: string | null;\n    address: string | null;\n    description: string | null;\n    facilities: string[] | null;\n    winterSports: boolean;\n    summerActivities: boolean;\n    altitude: string | null;\n    images: string[];\n await browser.close();\n}\n\nasync function fetchPageContent(url: string, waitForSelector?: string): Promise<string | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });\n        if (waitForSelector) {\n            await page.waitForSelector(waitForSelector, { timeout: 10000 });\n        }\n        const content = await page.content();\n        return content;\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching page content from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchSearchResults(url: string): Promise<{ propertyLinks: string[], jsonLd.description;\n                    data.images = jsonLd.image;\n                } catch(e) {\n                    console.error(\"Error parsing JSON-LD\", e);\n                }\n            }\n ‚ú® ## MODEL

The `properties.json` file is incomplete. My JSON-LD parsing isn't enough. I'll create a hybrid approach in `src/main.ts` to first try JSON-LD extraction, then use `page.evaluate()` with selectors to fill in missing data. I'll also re-enable the "Utforsk" link and image download logic for a more robust solution. I'm updating `src/main.ts` now.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import * as cheerio from 'cheerio';\nimport puppeteer from 'puppeteer';\nimport { Browser, Page } from 'puppeteer';\nimport * as fs from 'fs/promises';\n\nconst BASE_URL = \"https://www.finn.no/realestate/leisuresale/search.html?filters=\";\n\ninterface PropertyDetails {\n    url: string;\n    finnCode: string | null;\n    price: string | null;\n    address: string | null;\n    description: string | null;\n    facilities: string[] | null;\n    winterSports: boolean;\n    summerActivities: boolean;\n    altitude: string | null;\n    images: string[];\n    exploreLink: string | null;\n    exploreDetails?: any;\n}\n\nlet browser: Browser;\n\nasync function initializeBrowser() {\n    browser = await puppeteer.launch({ headless: true });\n}\n\nasync function closeBrowser() {\n    await browser.close();\n}\n\nasync function fetchPageContent(url: string, waitForSelector?: string): Promise<string | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'domcontentloaded' });\n        if (waitForSelector) {\n            await page.waitForSelector(waitForSelector, { timeout: 10000 });\n        }\n        const content = await page.content();\n        return content;\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching page content from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function fetchSearchResults(url: string): Promise<{ propertyLinks: string[], nextPageLink: string | null }> {\n    const propertyLinks: string[] = [];\n    let nextPageLink: string | null = null;\n\n    const content = await fetchPageContent(url, 'main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]');\n    if (!content) {\n        return { propertyLinks: [], nextPageLink: null };\n    }\n\n    const $ = cheerio.load(content);\n\n    $('main a[href*=\"ad.html?finnkode=\"]').each((i: number, element: any) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link && !propertyLinks.includes(link)) {\n            const fullLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            propertyLinks.push(fullLink);\n        }\n    });\n    console.log(`Found ${propertyLinks.length} property links on ${url}`);\n\n    $('nav[aria-label=\"Pagination\"] a[title=\"Neste side\"]').each((i: number, element: any) => {\n        const link = $(element).attr('href');\n        if (link) {\n            nextPageLink = link.startsWith('http') ? link : `https://www.finn.no${link}`;\n            return false;\n        }\n    });\n\n    return { propertyLinks, nextPageLink };\n}\n\nasync function fetchPropertyDetails(url: string): Promise<PropertyDetails | null> {\n    let page: Page | undefined;\n    try {\n        page = await browser.newPage();\n        await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'networkidle2' });\n\n        const details: PropertyDetails = await page.evaluate(() => {\n            const data: any = {};\n            const jsonLdElement = document.querySelector('script[type=\"application/ld+json\"]');\n            if (jsonLdElement) {\n                try {\n                    const jsonLd = JSON.parse(jsonLdElement.innerHTML);\n                    data.price = jsonLd.priceSpecification?.price.toString() || null;\n                    data.address = jsonLd.address?.streetAddress || null;\n                    data.description = jsonLd.description;\n                    data.images = jsonLd.image;\n                } catch(e) {\n                    console.error(\"Error parsing JSON-LD\", e);\n                }\n            }\n            \n            const getElementText = (selector: string) => document.querySelector(selector)?.textContent?.trim() || null;\n            \n            data.price = data.price || getElementText('div[data-testid=\"price-suggestion\"] dd');\n            data.address = data.address || getElementText('p[data-testid=\"object-address\"]');\n            data.description = data.description || getElementText('div.udt-description-text');\n\n            const facilities: string[] = [];\n            document.querySelectorAll('section[aria-labelledby=\"facilities-heading\"] dt').forEach(el => {\n                if (el.textContent) {\n                    facilities.push(el.textContent.trim());\n                }\n            });\n            data.facilities = facilities;\n            \n            let exploreLink: string | null = null;\n            const exploreLinks = document.querySelectorAll('section[aria-label=\"Om nabolaget\"] a');\n            for(const link of Array.from(exploreLinks)){\n                if(link.textContent?.trim() === \"Utforsk\"){\n                    exploreLink = (link as HTMLAnchorElement).href;\n                    break;\n                }\n            }\n            data.exploreLink = exploreLink;\n            \n            data.altitude = getElementText('div[data-testid=\"area-profile-property-item-altitude\"] dd');\n\n            return data;\n        });\n\n        const finnCodeMatch = url.match(/finnkode=(\\d+)/);\n        details.finnCode = finnCodeMatch ? finnCodeMatch[1] : null;\n        details.url = url;\n\n        let winterSports = false;\n        let summerActivities = false;\n\n        if (details.altitude) {\n            const altitudeValue = parseInt(details.altitude.replace(/[^0-9]/g, ''));\n            if (altitudeValue > 500) {\n                winterSports = true;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (details.facilities) {\n            if (details.facilities.some(f => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"bademulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"fiskemulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"strand\"))) {\n                summerActivities = true;\n            }\n            if (details.facilities.some(f => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"alpinanlegg\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"skil√∏ype\"))) {\n                winterSports = true;\n            }\n        }\n        details.winterSports = winterSports;\n        details.summerActivities = summerActivities;\n\n        return details;\n\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching property details from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nasync function scrapeAllPages(startUrl: string) {\n    await initializeBrowser();\n    let currentUrl: string | null = startUrl;\n    const allDetails: PropertyDetails[] = [];\n\n    try {\n        while (currentUrl) {\n            console.log(`Scraping page: ${currentUrl}`);\n            const { propertyLinks, nextPageLink } = await fetchSearchResults(currentUrl);\n\n            for (const link of propertyLinks) {\n                const details = await fetchPropertyDetails(link);\n                if (details) {\n                    allDetails.push(details);\n                }\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));\n            }\n\n            currentUrl = nextPageLink;\n            if (currentUrl) {\n                console.log(`Waiting for 1 second before fetching next page...`);\n                await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));\n            }\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allDetails.length} properties.`);\n        \n        await fs.writeFile('properties.json', JSON.stringify(allDetails, null, 2));\n        console.log('Saved data to properties.json');\n\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n",
    "file_path": "src/main.ts"
  }
}

description = ad.generalText.find((t: any) => t.heading === \"Kort om eiendommen\")?.textUnsafe || null;\n                \n                const facilities = ad.facilities;\n\n                let winterSports = false;\n                let summerActivities = false;\n                let altitude: string | null = null;\n\n                if (ad.location.altitude) {\n                    altitude = ad.location.altitude.toString();\n                    if (ad.location.altitude > 500) {\n                        winterSports = true;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (facilities.some((f: string) => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"bademulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"fiskemulighet\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"strand\"))) {\n                    summerActivities = true;\n                }\n                if (facilities.some((f: string) => f.toLowerCase().includes(\"alpinanlegg\") || f.toLowerCase().includes(\"skil√∏ype\"))) {\n                    winterSports = true;\n                }\n\n                const images = ad.images.map((m: any) => m.uri);\n                const exploreLink = ad.areaProfileUrl;\n\n                return {\n                    url: url,\n                    finnCode: finnCode,\n                    price: price,\n                    address: address,\n                    description: description,\n                    facilities: facilities.length > 0 ? facilities : null,\n                    winterSports: winterSports,\n                    summerActivities: summerActivities,\n                    altitude: altitude,\n                    images: images,\n                    exploreLink: exploreLink,\n                };\n\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error(\"Error parsing __NEXT_DATA__\", error);\n                return null;\n            }\n        }\n    } catch (error: any) {\n        console.error(`Error fetching property details from ${url}: ${error.message}`);\n        return null;\n    } finally {\n        if (page) {\n            await page.close();\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\nasync function scrapeAllPages(startUrl: string) {\n    await initializeBrowser();\n    let currentUrl: string | null = startUrl;\n    const allDetails: PropertyDetails[] = [];\n\n    try {\n        while (currentUrl) {\n            console.log(`Scraping page: ${currentUrl}`);\n            const { propertyLinks, nextPageLink } = await fetchSearchResults(currentUrl);\n\n            // Scrape only the first property for debugging\n            if (propertyLinks.length > 0) {\n                const details = await fetchPropertyDetails(propertyLinks[0]);\n                if (details) {\n                    allDetails.push(details);\n                }\n            }\n            break; // Stop after the first page for debugging\n\n        }\n        console.log(`Finished scraping. Found a total of ${allDetails.length} properties.`);\n        \n        await fs.writeFile('properties.json', JSON.stringify(allDetails, null, 2));\n        console.log('Saved data to properties.json');\n\n    } finally {\n        await closeBrowser();\n    }\n}\n\nscrapeAllPages(BASE_URL);\n",
    "file_path": "src/main.ts"
  }
}
